4678:vidvAn dEzwikatAm na Alambate pOruze ca na nizIdati ca
4679:kintu satkaviH SabdArTO iva dvayam apekzate
4680:rasasya sTAyinaH ekasya arTe BUyAMsaH saYcAriRaH BAvAH yaTA pravartante taTA sTAyinaH ekasya netuH arTe BUyAMsaH mahIBftaH pravartante ca
4681:tantrAvApavidA yogEH maRqalAni aDizWitA narendreRa SatravaH PaRIndrAH iva sunigrahAH Bavati ca
4682:uttuNgaH prajYAbalabfhanmUlaH utsAhapAdapaH karapraceyAm praTIyasIm praBuSaktim Palati
4683:diSAm jitvarEH BrAtfBiH karadIkftaBUpAlaH tapasaH sutaH asmat vinA api ijyAyE alam BUzRuH
4684:analpatvAt praDAnatvAt vaMSasya itare svarAH iva vijigIzoH nfpatayaH parivAratAm prayAnti
4685:anAraBamARasya api viBoH parEH utpAditAH arTAH vihAyasaH SabdAH iva guRatAm vrajanti
4686:ekArTatantuprotAyAm yAtavyapArzRigrAhAdimAlAyAm aDikadyutiH nAyakaH nAyakAyate
4687:SaktyapekzaH san zAqguRyam rasAyanam yuYjIta
4688:evam asya aNgAni sTAsnUni balavanti ca Bavanti
4689:sTAne SamavatAm aNginAm SaktyA vyAyAme vfdDiH Bavati
4690:ayaTAbalam AramBaH kzayasampadaH nidAnam Bavati
4691:tat tam cedInAm ISitAram BavAn mA avamaMsta
4692:yaH udAttaH svarAn iva arIn ekapade nihanti
4693:asO cedirAw ekaH ataH jetavyaH iti mA vedi
4694:yat saH rAjayakzmA rogARAm iva mahIBftAm samUhaH asti
4695:sampAditaPalaH sapakzaH paraBedanaH bARaH guRinA tena kArmukeRa iva sanDAnam ezyati
4696:ye ca anye kAlayavanaSAlvarukmidrumAdayaH svaBAvAH santi te api pradozam enam anuyAyinaH Bavanti ca
4697:tena kftaH alpaH api upajApaH tvayi AkopavataH tAn anilaH sAgnIn eDAn iva ASu dIpayitA
